For any of yâ€™all wondering, the guy playing synth in the corner is Daniel Lopatin, aka Oneohtrix Point Never. He was the co-executive producer on Dawn FM, plus has done some remixes (save your tears and Dawn FM are the two I think). He also was music director for Abelâ€™s halftime show a couple years back. Not only that, heâ€™s an incredible musician in his own right. Arguably a GOAT of experimental electronic music, inventor of vaporwave, did the soundtrack for Uncut Gems (where he and Abel met actually), and a quickly rising star of a producer. Abel was co-executive producer on his most recent album, plus provided the vocals for No Nightmares, which is an incredible song.
